{\footnotesize\ttfamily bool Joy\+Button\+::is\+Part\+Real\+Axis (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [virtual]}}



Check if button should be considered a part of a real controller axis. Needed for some dialogs so the program won\textquotesingle{}t have to resort to type checking. 

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
Status of being part of a real controller axis 
\end{DoxyReturn}
